\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01067}01067                 v = params \% csph(:, isph) -\/ params \% csph(:, jsph) + \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01068}01068                     \& params \% rsph(isph)*constants \% cgrid(:, igrid)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01069}01069                 maxv = max(abs(v(1)), abs(v(2)), abs(v(3)))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01070}01070                 ssqv = (v(1)/maxv)**2 + (v(2)/maxv)**2 + (v(3)/maxv)**2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01071}01071                 vv = maxv * sqrt(ssqv)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01292}01292         constants \% inl(isph) = lnl + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01293}01293         inode = constants \% snode(isph)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01294}01294         \textcolor{comment}{! loop over near clusters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01295}01295         \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} j = constants \% snear(inode), constants \% snear(inode+1) -\/ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01296}01296             jnode = constants \% near(j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01297}01297             \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} k = constants \% cluster(1, jnode), constants \% cluster(2, jnode)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01298}01298                 jsph = constants \% order(k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01299}01299                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (isph .ne. jsph) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01302}01302                     ssqv = (v(1)/maxv)**2 + (v(2)/maxv)**2 + (v(3)/maxv)**2}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01307}01307                     \textcolor{comment}{! switching region as we need a symmetric neighbor list to}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01486}01486     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x .le. flow) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01487}01487         \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a66fd73de84672f0f78f4c9c4e2c620b5}{dfsw}} = zero}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01488}01488     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01489}01489         \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a66fd73de84672f0f78f4c9c4e2c620b5}{dfsw}} = -\/f30 * (( (one-\/x)*(x-\/one+eta) )**2) / (eta**5)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01490}01490 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01491}01491 \textcolor{keyword}{end function }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a66fd73de84672f0f78f4c9c4e2c620b5}{dfsw}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01492}01492 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01497}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a5d1fc3f2c16984ceaa0e1ed9de8fb548}{01497}} \textcolor{keyword}{subroutine }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a5d1fc3f2c16984ceaa0e1ed9de8fb548}{mkprec}}(lmax, nbasis, nsph, ngrid, eps, ui, wgrid, vgrid, \&}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01502}01502         \& vgrid(vgrid\_nbasis, ngrid)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01503}01503     \textcolor{comment}{!! Output}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01504}01504 \textcolor{keywordtype}{    real}(dp), \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(out)} :: rx\_prc(nbasis, nbasis, nsph)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01506}01506     \textcolor{keywordtype}{character(len=255)}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(out)} :: error\_message}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01508}01508     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer} :: isph, lm, ind, l1, m1, ind1, igrid}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01509}01509 \textcolor{keywordtype}{    real}(dp)  :: f, f1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01510}01510     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{allocatable} :: ipiv(:)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01511}01511 \textcolor{keywordtype}{    real}(dp),  \textcolor{keywordtype}{allocatable} :: work(:)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01512}01512     \textcolor{keywordtype}{external} :: dgetrf, dgetri}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01513}01513     \textcolor{comment}{! Allocation of temporaries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01514}01514     \textcolor{keyword}{allocate}(ipiv(nbasis), work(nbasis**2), stat=info)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01515}01515     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (info .ne. 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01516}01516         error\_message = \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}mkprec: `ipiv` and `work` allocation failed"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01517}01517         info = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01518}01518         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01519}01519 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01520}01520     \textcolor{comment}{! Init}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01521}01521     rx\_prc = zero}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01522}01522     \textcolor{comment}{! Off-\/diagonal part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01523}01523     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} isph = 1, nsph}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01524}01524         \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} igrid = 1, ngrid}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01525}01525             f = twopi * ui(igrid, isph) * wgrid(igrid)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01526}01526             \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} l1 = 0, lmax}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01527}01527                 ind1 = l1*l1 + l1 + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01528}01528                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} m1 = -\/l1, l1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01529}01529                     f1 = f * vgrid(ind1+m1, igrid) / (two*dble(l1) + one)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01530}01530                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} lm = 1, nbasis}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01531}01531                         rx\_prc(lm, ind1+m1, isph) = \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01532}01532                             \& rx\_prc(lm, ind1+m1, isph) + f1*vgrid(lm, igrid)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01533}01533 \textcolor{keywordflow}{                    end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01534}01534 \textcolor{keywordflow}{                end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01535}01535 \textcolor{keywordflow}{            end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01536}01536 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01537}01537 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01538}01538     \textcolor{comment}{! add diagonal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01539}01539     f = twopi * (eps+one) / (eps-\/one)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01540}01540     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} isph = 1, nsph}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01541}01541         \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} lm = 1, nbasis}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01542}01542             rx\_prc(lm, lm, isph) = rx\_prc(lm, lm, isph) + f}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01543}01543 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01544}01544 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01545}01545     \textcolor{comment}{! invert the blocks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01546}01546     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} isph = 1, nsph}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01547}01547         \textcolor{keyword}{call }dgetrf(nbasis, nbasis, rx\_prc(:, :, isph), nbasis, ipiv, info)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01548}01548         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (info .ne. 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then} }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01549}01549             error\_message = \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}mkprec: dgetrf failed"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01550}01550             info = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01551}01551             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01552}01552 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01553}01553         \textcolor{keyword}{call }dgetri(nbasis, rx\_prc(:, :, isph), nbasis, ipiv, work, \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01554}01554             \& nbasis**2, info)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01555}01555         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (info .ne. 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then} }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01556}01556             error\_message = \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}mkprec: dgetri failed"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01557}01557             info = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01558}01558             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01559}01559 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01560}01560 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01561}01561     \textcolor{comment}{! Cleanup temporaries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01562}01562     \textcolor{keyword}{deallocate}(work, ipiv, stat=info)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01563}01563     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (info .ne. 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01567}01567 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01568}01568   \textcolor{comment}{! Cleanup error message if there were no error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01569}01569     error\_message = \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01570}01570 \textcolor{keyword}{end subroutine }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a5d1fc3f2c16984ceaa0e1ed9de8fb548}{mkprec}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01571}01571 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01593}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a71a53ad578c20da9306b93deda562aeb}{01593}} \textcolor{keyword}{subroutine }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a71a53ad578c20da9306b93deda562aeb}{tree\_rib\_build}}(nsph, csph, rsph, order, cluster, children, parent, \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01594}01594         \& cnode, rnode, snode)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01595}01595     \textcolor{comment}{! Inputs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01596}01596     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)} :: nsph}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01597}01597 \textcolor{keywordtype}{    real}(dp), \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)} :: csph(3, nsph), rsph(nsph)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01598}01598     \textcolor{comment}{! Outputs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01599}01599     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(out)} :: order(nsph), cluster(2, 2*nsph-\/1), \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01600}01600         \& children(2, 2*nsph-\/1), parent(2*nsph-\/1), snode(nsph)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01601}01601     \textcolor{keywordtype}{real(dp)}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(out)} :: cnode(3, 2*nsph-\/1), rnode(2*nsph-\/1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01602}01602     \textcolor{comment}{! Local variables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01603}01603     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer} :: nclusters, i, j, n, s, e, div}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01604}01604 \textcolor{keywordtype}{    real}(dp) :: r, r1, r2, c(3), c1(3), c2(3), d, maxc, ssqc}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01605}01605     \textcolor{comment}{!! At first construct the tree}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01606}01606     nclusters = 2*nsph -\/ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01607}01607     \textcolor{comment}{! Init the root node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01608}01608     cluster(1, 1) = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01609}01609     cluster(2, 1) = nsph}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01610}01610     parent(1) = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01611}01611     \textcolor{comment}{! Index of the first unassigned node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01612}01612     j = 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01613}01613     \textcolor{comment}{! Init spheres ordering}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01614}01614     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i = 1, nsph}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01615}01615         order(i) = i}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01616}01616 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01617}01617     \textcolor{comment}{! Divide nodes until a single spheres}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01618}01618     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i = 1, nclusters}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01619}01619         \textcolor{comment}{! The first sphere in i-\/th node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01620}01620         s = cluster(1, i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01621}01621         \textcolor{comment}{! The last sphere in i-\/th node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01622}01622         e = cluster(2, i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01623}01623         \textcolor{comment}{! Number of spheres in i-\/th node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01624}01624         n = e -\/ s + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01625}01625         \textcolor{comment}{! Divide only if there are 2 or more spheres}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01626}01626         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (n .gt. 1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01627}01627             \textcolor{comment}{! Use inertial bisection to reorder spheres and cut into 2 halfs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01628}01628             \textcolor{keyword}{call }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a7c5d6aebc32c85aa05d4a74678ff95f7}{tree\_rib\_node\_bisect}}(nsph, csph, n, order(s:e), div)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01629}01629             \textcolor{comment}{! Assign the first half to the j-\/th node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01630}01630             cluster(1, j) = s}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01631}01631             cluster(2, j) = s + div -\/ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01632}01632             \textcolor{comment}{! Assign the second half to the (j+1)-\/th node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01633}01633             cluster(1, j+1) = s + div}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01634}01634             cluster(2, j+1) = e}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01635}01635             \textcolor{comment}{! Update list of children of i-\/th node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01636}01636             children(1, i) = j}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01637}01637             children(2, i) = j + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01638}01638             \textcolor{comment}{! Set parents of new j-\/th and (j+1)-\/th node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01639}01639             parent(j) = i}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01640}01640             parent(j+1) = i}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01641}01641             \textcolor{comment}{! Shift index of the first unassigned node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01642}01642             j = j + 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01643}01643         \textcolor{comment}{! Set information for a leaf node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01644}01644         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01645}01645             \textcolor{comment}{! No children nodes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01646}01646             children(:, i) = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01647}01647             \textcolor{comment}{! i-\/th node contains sphere ind(s)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01648}01648             snode(order(s)) = i}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01649}01649 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01650}01650 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01651}01651     \textcolor{comment}{!! Compute bounding spheres of each node of the tree}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01652}01652     \textcolor{comment}{! Bottom-\/to-\/top pass over all nodes of the tree}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01653}01653     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i = nclusters, 1, -\/1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01654}01654         \textcolor{comment}{! In case of a leaf node just use corresponding input sphere as a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01655}01655         \textcolor{comment}{! bounding sphere of the node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01656}01656         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (children(1, i) .eq. 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01657}01657             \textcolor{comment}{! Get correct index of the corresponding input sphere}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01658}01658             j = order(cluster(1, i))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01659}01659             \textcolor{comment}{! Get corresponding center and radius}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01660}01660             cnode(:, i) = csph(:, j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01661}01661             rnode(i) = rsph(j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01662}01662         \textcolor{comment}{! In case of a non-\/leaf node get minimal sphere that contains bounding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01663}01663         \textcolor{comment}{! spheres of children nodes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01664}01664         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01665}01665             \textcolor{comment}{! The first child}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01666}01666             j = children(1, i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01667}01667             c1 = cnode(:, j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01668}01668             r1 = rnode(j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01669}01669             \textcolor{comment}{! The second child}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01670}01670             j = children(2, i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01671}01671             c2 = cnode(:, j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01672}01672             r2 = rnode(j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01673}01673             \textcolor{comment}{! Distance between centers of bounding spheres of children nodes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01674}01674             c = c1 -\/ c2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01675}01675             \textcolor{comment}{! Compute distance by scale and sum of scaled squares}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01676}01676             maxc = max(abs(c(1)), abs(c(2)), abs(c(3)))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01677}01677             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (maxc .eq. zero) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01678}01678                 d = zero}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01679}01679             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01680}01680                 d = (c(1)/maxc)**2 + (c(2)/maxc)**2 + (c(3)/maxc)**2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01681}01681                 d = maxc * sqrt(d)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01682}01682 \textcolor{keywordflow}{            end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01683}01683             \textcolor{comment}{! If sphere \#2 is completely inside sphere \#1 use the first sphere}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01684}01684             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r1 .ge. (r2+d)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01685}01685                 c = c1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01686}01686                 r = r1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01687}01687             \textcolor{comment}{! If sphere \#1 is completely inside sphere \#2 use the second sphere}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01688}01688             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(r2 .ge. (r1+d)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01689}01689                 c = c2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01690}01690                 r = r2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01691}01691             \textcolor{comment}{! Otherwise use special formula to find a minimal sphere}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01692}01692             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01693}01693                 r = (r1+r2+d) / 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01694}01694                 c = c2 + c/d*(r-\/r2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01695}01695 \textcolor{keywordflow}{            end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01696}01696             \textcolor{comment}{! Assign computed bounding sphere}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01697}01697             cnode(:, i) = c}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01698}01698             rnode(i) = r}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01699}01699 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01700}01700 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01701}01701 \textcolor{keyword}{end subroutine }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a71a53ad578c20da9306b93deda562aeb}{tree\_rib\_build}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01702}01702 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01712}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a7c5d6aebc32c85aa05d4a74678ff95f7}{01712}} \textcolor{keyword}{subroutine }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a7c5d6aebc32c85aa05d4a74678ff95f7}{tree\_rib\_node\_bisect}}(nsph, csph, n, order, div)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01713}01713     \textcolor{comment}{! Inputs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01714}01714     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)} :: nsph, n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01715}01715 \textcolor{keywordtype}{    real}(dp), \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)} :: csph(3, nsph)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01716}01716     \textcolor{comment}{! Outputs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01717}01717     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(inout)} :: order(n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01718}01718     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(out)} :: div}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01719}01719     \textcolor{comment}{! Local variables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01720}01720 \textcolor{keywordtype}{    real}(dp) :: c(3),  s(3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01721}01721 \textcolor{keywordtype}{    real}(dp), \textcolor{keywordtype}{allocatable} :: tmp\_csph(:, :), work(:)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01722}01722     \textcolor{keywordtype}{external} :: dgesvd}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01723}01723     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer} :: i, l, r, lwork, info, istat}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01724}01724     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{allocatable} :: tmp\_order(:)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01725}01725 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01726}01726     \textcolor{keyword}{allocate}(tmp\_csph(3, n), tmp\_order(n), stat=istat)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01727}01727     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (istat .ne. 0) stop \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}allocation failed"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01728}01728 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01729}01729     \textcolor{comment}{! Get average coordinate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01730}01730     c = zero}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01731}01731     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i = 1, n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01732}01732         c = c + csph(:, order(i))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01733}01733 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01734}01734     c = c / n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01735}01735     \textcolor{comment}{! Get coordinates minus average in a contiguous array}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01736}01736     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i = 1, n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01737}01737         tmp\_csph(:, i) = csph(:, order(i)) -\/ c}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01738}01738 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01739}01739     \textcolor{comment}{!! Find right singular vectors}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01740}01740     \textcolor{comment}{! Get proper size of temporary workspace}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01741}01741     lwork = -\/1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01742}01742     \textcolor{keyword}{call }dgesvd(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'N'}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{'O'}, 3, n, tmp\_csph, 3, s, tmp\_csph, 3, tmp\_csph, 3, \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01743}01743         \& s, lwork, info)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01744}01744     lwork = int(s(1))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01745}01745     \textcolor{keyword}{allocate}(work(lwork), stat=istat)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01746}01746     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (istat .ne. 0) stop \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}allocation failed"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01747}01747     \textcolor{comment}{! Get right singular vectors}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01748}01748     \textcolor{keyword}{call }dgesvd(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'N'}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{'O'}, 3, n, tmp\_csph, 3, s, tmp\_csph, 3, tmp\_csph, 3, \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01749}01749         \& work, lwork, info)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01750}01750     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (info .ne. 0) stop \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}dgesvd did not converge"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01751}01751     \textcolor{keyword}{deallocate}(work, stat=istat)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01752}01752     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (istat .ne. 0) stop \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}deallocation failed"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01753}01753     \textcolor{comment}{!! Sort spheres by sign of the above scalar product, which is equal to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01754}01754     \textcolor{comment}{!! the leading right singular vector scaled by the leading singular value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01755}01755     \textcolor{comment}{!! However, we only care about sign, so we take into account only the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01756}01756     \textcolor{comment}{!! leading right singular vector.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01757}01757     \textcolor{comment}{! First empty index from the left}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01758}01758     l = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01759}01759     \textcolor{comment}{! First empty index from the right}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01760}01760     r = n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01761}01761     \textcolor{comment}{! Cycle over values of the singular vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01762}01762     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i = 1, n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01763}01763         \textcolor{comment}{! Positive scalar products are moved to the beginning of `order`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01764}01764         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tmp\_csph(1, i) .ge. zero) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01765}01765             tmp\_order(l) = order(i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01766}01766             l = l + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01767}01767         \textcolor{comment}{! Negative scalar products are moved to the end of `order`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01768}01768         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01769}01769             tmp\_order(r) = order(i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01770}01770             r = r -\/ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01771}01771 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01772}01772 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01773}01773     \textcolor{comment}{! Set divider and update order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01774}01774     div = r}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01775}01775     order = tmp\_order}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01776}01776     \textcolor{keyword}{deallocate}(tmp\_csph, tmp\_order, stat=istat)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01777}01777     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (istat .ne. 0) stop \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}deallocation failed"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01778}01778 \textcolor{keyword}{end subroutine }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a7c5d6aebc32c85aa05d4a74678ff95f7}{tree\_rib\_node\_bisect}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01779}01779 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01804}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a3e9f0301398a1007b912f94c7239dffd}{01804}} \textcolor{keyword}{subroutine }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceddx__constants_a3e9f0301398a1007b912f94c7239dffd}{tree\_get\_farnear\_work}}(n, children, cnode, rnode, lwork, iwork, \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01805}01805         \& jwork, work, nnfar, nfar, nnnear, nnear)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01806}01806     \textcolor{comment}{! Inputs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01807}01807     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)} :: n, children(2, n), lwork}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01808}01808 \textcolor{keywordtype}{    real}(dp), \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)} :: cnode(3, n), rnode(n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01809}01809     \textcolor{comment}{! Outputs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01810}01810     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(inout)} :: iwork, jwork, work(3, lwork)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01811}01811     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(out)} :: nnfar, nfar(n), nnnear, nnear(n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01812}01812     \textcolor{comment}{! Local variables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01813}01813     \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer} :: j(2), npairs, k1, k2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01814}01814 \textcolor{keywordtype}{    real}(dp) :: c(3), r, d, dmax, dssq}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01815}01815     \textcolor{comment}{! iwork is current temporary item in work array to process}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01816}01816     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (iwork .eq. 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01817}01817         work(1, 1) = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01818}01818         work(2, 1) = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01819}01819         iwork = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01820}01820         jwork = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01821}01821 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01822}01822     \textcolor{comment}{! jwork is total amount of temporary items in work array}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01823}01823     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (iwork .le. jwork)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01824}01824         j = work(1:2, iwork)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01825}01825         c = cnode(:, j(1)) -\/ cnode(:, j(2))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01826}01826         r = rnode(j(1)) + rnode(j(2)) + max(rnode(j(1)), rnode(j(2)))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01827}01827         \textcolor{comment}{!r = rnode(j(1)) + rnode(j(2))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01828}01828         dmax = max(abs(c(1)), abs(c(2)), abs(c(3)))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01829}01829         dssq = (c(1)/dmax)**2 + (c(2)/dmax)**2 + (c(3)/dmax)**2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01830}01830         d = dmax * sqrt(dssq)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01831}01831         \textcolor{comment}{!d = sqrt(c(1)**2 + c(2)**2 + c(3)**2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01832}01832         \textcolor{comment}{! If node has no children then assume itself for purpose of finding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01833}01833         \textcolor{comment}{! far-\/field and near-\/filed interactions with children nodes of another}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01834}01834         \textcolor{comment}{! node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01835}01835         npairs = max(1, children(2, j(1))-\/children(1, j(1))+1) * \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01836}01836             \& max(1, children(2, j(2))-\/children(1, j(2))+1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01837}01837         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (d .ge. r) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01838}01838             \textcolor{comment}{! Mark as far admissible pair}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01839}01839             work(3, iwork) = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01840}01840         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (npairs .eq. 1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01841}01841             \textcolor{comment}{! Mark as near admissible pair if both nodes are leaves}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01842}01842             work(3, iwork) = 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01843}01843         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (jwork+npairs .gt. lwork) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01844}01844             \textcolor{comment}{! Exit procedure, since work array was too small}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01845}01845             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01846}01846         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01847}01847             \textcolor{comment}{! Mark as non-\/admissible pair and check all pairs of children nodes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01848}01848             \textcolor{comment}{! or pairs of one node (if it is a leaf node) with children of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01849}01849             \textcolor{comment}{! another node}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01850}01850             work(3, iwork) = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01851}01851             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (children(1, j(1)) .eq. 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01852}01852                 k1 = j(1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01853}01853                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} k2 = children(1, j(2)), children(2, j(2))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01854}01854                     jwork = jwork + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01855}01855                     work(1, jwork) = k1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01856}01856                     work(2, jwork) = k2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01857}01857 \textcolor{keywordflow}{                end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01858}01858             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(children(1, j(2)) .eq. 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01859}01859                 k2 = j(2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01860}01860                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} k1 = children(1, j(1)), children(2, j(1))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01861}01861                     jwork = jwork + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01862}01862                     work(1, jwork) = k1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01863}01863                     work(2, jwork) = k2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01864}01864 \textcolor{keywordflow}{                end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01865}01865             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01866}01866                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} k1 = children(1, j(1)), children(2, j(1))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01867}01867                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} k2 = children(1, j(2)), children(2, j(2))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01868}01868                         jwork = jwork + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01869}01869                         work(1, jwork) = k1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01870}01870                         work(2, jwork) = k2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01871}01871 \textcolor{keywordflow}{                    end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01872}01872 \textcolor{keywordflow}{                end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01873}01873 \textcolor{keywordflow}{            end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01874}01874 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01875}01875         iwork = iwork + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{ddx__constants_8f90_source_l01876}01876 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    end do}}
